Our findings suggest that prompt design and activation steering should be jointly optimized for culturally aware multilingual inference.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在多樣的語言和文化背景中越來越被廣泛使用，但它們的文化知識在不同地區和語言之間仍然不均衡。我們提出了DFKI-MLT系統，用於SemEval-2026第7任務的文化意識，在此我們利用從平行FLORES數據中提取的語言向量對多語言LLMs進行激活引導。我們的方法通過在選定的Transformer層中將語言特定的引導向量添加到殘差流中來執行推理時的適應，而無需任何參數更新。我們參加了短答案（SAQ）和多選題（MCQ）兩個賽道；然而，只有我們的MCQ提交獲得了官方分數。在官方MCQ賽道中，我們達到了86.96%的準確率，排名17支隊伍中的第7位。為了更好地理解系統行為，我們對共享任務的MCQ和SAQ設置進行了事後分析。這些分析顯示，激活引導在文化推理上產生了適度且異質的改善：增益對層次非常敏感，在語言-地區對之間變化顯著，某些配置甚至會降低性能，並且與提示的制定互動，對比通用和文化條件提示。我們的發現表明，提示設計和激活引導應該共同優化，以實現文化意識的多語言推理。

##### **Do Language Models Know What Not to Say? Causal Evidence for Statistical Preemption in LLMs**
2605.23039v1 by Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu

How do learners acquire knowledge of what is unacceptable without negative evidence? Construction Grammar proposes statistical preemption: exposure to a conventional form (e.g., "donated the books to the library") preempts structurally possible but unattested alternatives ("*donated the library the books"). We present a computational study that, for the first time, directly dissociates statistical preemption from the competing entrenchment hypothesis in large language models within a single converging design. Across four experiments spanning 120 English verb-construction pairings (dative, causative, locative), we show that (1) LLM surprisal patterns correlate strongly with human acceptability judgments ($r = 0.79$), validated against three independent behavioral datasets; (2) these patterns are driven by competing-form frequency rather than overall verb frequency, confirmed by non-circular partial correlations; (3) preemption sensitivity scales as a power law with model size; and (4) a controlled fine-tuning intervention causally demonstrates that manipulating competing-form frequencies shifts preemption behavior in the predicted direction, with reverse-direction controls ruling out frequency-sensitivity confounds. These results provide converging evidence that neural language models acquire negative linguistic knowledge through distributional competition, the core mechanism posited by Construction Grammar.

摘要：學習者如何在沒有負面證據的情況下獲得對不可接受內容的知識？建構語法提出了統計預先排除的概念：接觸到一種慣用形式（例如，“將書籍捐贈給圖書館”）會預先排除結構上可能但未被證實的替代形式（“*將圖書館捐贈書籍”）。我們呈現了一項計算研究，首次在單一的收斂設計中直接將統計預先排除與競爭固著假設區分開來。在四個實驗中，涵蓋了120對英語動詞-結構配對（受益、使役、位置），我們顯示（1）LLM的驚訝模式與人類可接受性判斷之間有強烈的相關性（$r = 0.79$），並通過三個獨立的行為數據集進行了驗證；（2）這些模式是由競爭形式的頻率驅動，而非整體動詞頻率，這一點通過非循環的部分相關性得到了確認；（3）預先排除的敏感度隨著模型大小呈冪律增長；（4）一項受控的微調干預因果證明，操控競爭形式的頻率會在預測的方向上改變預先排除行為，並且反向控制排除了頻率敏感的混淆因素。這些結果提供了收斂的證據，表明神經語言模型通過分佈競爭獲得負面語言知識，這是建構語法所假設的核心機制。

##### **Uncovering the Latent Potential of Deep Intermediate Representations**
2605.23033v1 by Arnesh Batra, Arush Gumber, Aniket Khandelwal, Jashn Khemani, Anubha Gupta

Foundational Models pretrained on huge amount of data learn representations that evolve across depth, forming a hierarchy of embeddings with distinct semantic content and geometric structure. Contrary to the widespread practice of using only the final layer or shallow mixtures, we show that task-relevant information is distributed non-monotonically across layers and cannot be recovered by naïve aggregation. Through a geometric and empirical study across multiple modalities, we show that effective transfer depends on identifying which layers encode task-discriminative structure and how their embeddings are geometrically organized. We introduce Layer-wise Optimal Embedding Selection (LOES), a constructive spectral method that identifies task-discriminative subspaces by minimizing residual error under orthogonality and isotropy constraints. To align fine-tuning with this selection principle, we further propose Geometric Regularization Loss (GeoReg), which enforces a simplicial structure on class manifolds and stabilizes representation geometry during fine-tuning. Across a wide range of architectures, depths, modalities, and data regimes, LOES consistently outperforms standard baselines, with gains that grow as model depth increases. Beyond accuracy, our method reveals how semantic factors are distributed across layers, thereby enabling cross-lingual and cross-modal interpretability analyses. Together, our results provide strong evidence that layerwise embedding geometry is not incidental but central to how deep models represent and transfer knowledge.

摘要：基礎模型在大量數據上預訓練，學習的表示隨著深度而演變，形成具有不同語義內容和幾何結構的嵌入層次。與普遍只使用最終層或淺層混合的做法相反，我們展示了與任務相關的信息在層之間以非單調方式分佈，並且無法通過天真的聚合來恢復。通過對多種模態進行幾何和實證研究，我們表明有效的轉移依賴於識別哪些層編碼了任務區分結構以及它們的嵌入是如何在幾何上組織的。我們引入了層級最佳嵌入選擇（LOES），這是一種建設性的光譜方法，通過在正交性和各向同性約束下最小化殘差誤差來識別任務區分子空間。為了使微調與這一選擇原則對齊，我們進一步提出了幾何正則化損失（GeoReg），該方法在類別流形上強制執行簡單結構，並在微調過程中穩定表示幾何。在各種架構、深度、模態和數據範疇中，LOES 一直優於標準基準，並且隨著模型深度的增加而增長的增益。除了準確性，我們的方法還揭示了語義因素在層之間的分佈，從而使跨語言和跨模態的可解釋性分析成為可能。總體而言，我們的結果提供了強有力的證據，表明層級嵌入幾何不是偶然的，而是深度模型如何表示和轉移知識的核心。

##### **The Deterministic Horizon: Impossibility Results as Design Specifications for Trustworthy AI Systems**
2605.23024v1 by Dongxin Guo

Large language models now write software, draft legal documents, and produce clinical notes, yet fundamental limits, from Turing and Arrow to the No Free Lunch theorems, shape what computation can do. This thesis turns such impossibility results from curiosities into design rules. Its flagship result proves an accuracy ceiling set by architecture alone: past a critical reasoning depth, no amount of training moves it, at any adapter rank, sample size, or loss function. Computable before deployment from layer count and embedding width, this Deterministic Horizon is measured between nineteen and thirty-one across twelve transformer architectures, and fine-tuning on optimal-length traces recovers under four percentage points. The mechanism is a capacity invariant of the residual stream, and an information-theoretic conversion yields super-exponential accuracy decay past the horizon. An unconditional circuit-complexity lower bound for modular exponentiation against constant-depth prime-modulus circuits complements this result. The same argument recasts across subfields: preference learning under any misspecified model jumps discontinuously in sample complexity; multi-stage retrieval pipelines require at least as many independent metrics as stages; standard truthful auctions fail for agents with prompt-dependent valuations; and zero-knowledge verification of neural inference pays a measured overhead of one hundred ten to one hundred ninety times per non-linear activation. Together these form a catalogue of sixteen specifications, each pairing a computable boundary, a quantified violation cost, and a constructive design rule: two compositions are proved, one pairing is an honest obstruction, and four remain open. The impossibility-specification methodology is offered for the generative research programme that trustworthy AI may need. Every fundamental limit of AI is also a design rule.

摘要：大型語言模型現在能夠編寫軟體、起草法律文件和產生臨床筆記，但從圖靈到阿羅以及無免費午餐定理的基本限制，塑造了計算能做的事情。這篇論文將這些不可能的結果從好奇心轉化為設計規則。其旗艦結果證明了一個僅由架構設定的準確性上限：在關鍵推理深度之後，無論訓練多少，都無法改變它，無論是適配器等級、樣本大小還是損失函數。在部署之前，這個確定性地平線可以從層數和嵌入寬度計算出來，並且在十二種Transformer架構中測量介於十九到三十一之間，對最佳長度的追蹤進行微調可恢復不到四個百分點。這個機制是殘差流的容量不變性，信息理論的轉換在地平線之後產生超指數的準確性衰減。針對常數深度質數模電路的模塊指數運算的無條件電路複雜度下限補充了這一結果。同樣的論點在子領域中重新表述：在任何錯誤指定的模型下，偏好學習的樣本複雜度不連續跳躍；多階段檢索管道需要至少與階段數相同的獨立度量；標準的真實拍賣對於具有提示依賴估值的代理失效；而神經推理的零知識驗證每個非線性激活的測量開銷為一百十到一百九十倍。這些共同形成了一個十六項規範的目錄，每一項都配對了一個可計算邊界、一個量化的違規成本和一個建設性的設計規則：證明了兩個組合，一個配對是一個誠實的障礙，還有四個保持開放。這種不可能性規範方法論被提供給可信的人工智慧可能需要的生成研究計劃。人工智慧的每一個基本限制也是一條設計規則。

##### **Can AI Guess What You Know? Performance Comparison of Large Language Models for Human Domain Knowledge Estimation From Communication Logs**
2605.22971v1 by Ko Watanabe, Shoya Ishimaru

Employees often struggle to identify ``who knows what,'' leading to organizational productivity losses. We investigate whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can infer individual domain knowledge directly from long-term Slack logs. Analyzing 27,188 messages from 43 users, we evaluated seven models (including Gemini, Claude, and GPT families) by comparing their zero-shot estimates against self-reported skill ratings from 27 participants. Gemini 2.5 Flash achieved the lowest error (MAE 21.13%), while GPT models showed significantly larger discrepancies. Notably, estimation accuracy depended only weakly on message volume, indicating that more text alone does not guarantee better inference. These findings demonstrate the feasibility and current limits of automated expertise mapping, highlighting the need for privacy-preserving deployments and richer, structure-aware representations of human knowledge.

摘要：員工常常難以識別「誰知道什麼」，導致組織生產力損失。我們調查了大型語言模型（LLMs）是否能直接從長期的Slack日誌中推斷個體的領域知識。分析了43名用戶的27,188條消息，我們評估了七個模型（包括Gemini、Claude和GPT系列），通過將它們的零-shot估計與27名參與者的自我報告技能評級進行比較。Gemini 2.5 Flash實現了最低的誤差（MAE 21.13%），而GPT模型顯示出顯著更大的差異。值得注意的是，估計準確性僅與消息量有弱相關，這表明僅僅更多的文本並不保證更好的推斷。這些發現展示了自動專業知識映射的可行性和當前限制，突顯了對於保護隱私的部署和更豐富、結構感知的人類知識表示的需求。

##### **Graph Alignment Topology as an Inductive Bias for Grounding Detection**
2605.22963v1 by Paul Landes, Pranav Herur, Adam Cross, Jimeng Sun

Large Language Models (LLMs) are optimized to produce distributionally plausible continuations rather than to explicitly verify whether generated propositions are entailed by source documents. This inductive bias enables generalization, but it does not encode whether responses are grounded with respect to a reference. These issues limit the use of LLMs in domains where strict factual correctness is crucial, such as clinical decision support. Existing hallucination detection approaches improve factuality through retrieval augmentation, self-consistency, or claim verification, but generally do not learn directly over alignment topology. To leverage alignment topology as an inductive bias, we construct aligned bipartite graphs between reference information and LLM outputs and train a graph neural network (GNN) to model alignment structure using message passing. The method achieves state-of-the-art results on four diverse hallucination and question-answering datasets, outperforming all compared methods, including foundational LLMs such as GPT-4o.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）被優化為產生在分佈上合理的延續，而不是明確驗證生成的命題是否由源文件所推導。這種歸納偏見使得泛化成為可能，但它並不編碼回應是否與參考資料相符。這些問題限制了LLMs在對事實正確性要求嚴格的領域中的應用，例如臨床決策支持。現有的幻覺檢測方法通過檢索增強、自我一致性或主張驗證來提高事實性，但通常不直接在對齊拓撲上進行學習。為了利用對齊拓撲作為歸納偏見，我們在參考信息和LLM輸出之間構建對齊的二分圖，並訓練一個圖神經網絡（GNN）來使用消息傳遞建模對齊結構。該方法在四個不同的幻覺和問答數據集上達到了最先進的結果，超越了所有比較的方法，包括基礎的LLMs，如GPT-4o。

##### **RAS: Reflection-Augmented Scaling with In-Context Learning for Executable Cypher Query Generation**
2605.22937v1 by Minseok Jung, Abhas Ricky, Muhammad Rameez Chatni

Inference-time scaling can reduce errors in structured query generation, but methods to allocate the compute for query code generation remains underexplored. We study Text2Cypher, where language models generate Cypher queries that execute against property graph databases. Non-executable queries constitute a distinct syntactic failure separate from semantic inaccuracy: a syntax error triggers a system-generated error message from the database. These error messages are typically discarded at inference time rather than leveraged through in-context learning (ICL). We compare two inference methods: Independent Scaling (IS), which performs memoryless resampling, and Reflection-Augmented Scaling (RAS), which conditions each new attempt on prior execution feedback via ICL. Across three Neo4j datasets and five code-specialized language models, RAS reduces the Query Execution Error Rate by 41--50% at n{=}5, outperforming IS at 32--38%. Execution errors are not merely failures to discard but actionable feedback, and structuring inference-time compute around them is a more efficient path to executability than scaling independent samples.

摘要：推理時間的擴展可以減少結構化查詢生成中的錯誤，但分配查詢代碼生成計算的方法仍然未被充分探索。我們研究了 Text2Cypher，該模型使語言模型生成可對屬性圖數據庫執行的 Cypher 查詢。不可執行的查詢構成了一種獨特的語法失敗，與語義不準確性分開：語法錯誤會觸發數據庫生成的系統錯誤消息。這些錯誤消息通常在推理時被丟棄，而不是通過上下文學習（ICL）加以利用。我們比較了兩種推理方法：獨立擴展（IS），它執行無記憶的重採樣，以及反射增強擴展（RAS），它根據先前執行反饋通過 ICL 條件化每次新的嘗試。在三個 Neo4j 數據集和五個專門的代碼語言模型中，RAS 將查詢執行錯誤率降低了 41--50%（n{=}5），在 32--38% 的範圍內超越了 IS。執行錯誤不僅僅是丟棄的失敗，而是可操作的反饋，圍繞這些錯誤結構化推理時間計算比擴展獨立樣本是一條更有效的執行路徑。

##### **AI-Friendly LaTeX: Using LaTeX Code as a Knowledge Source for Retrieval-Augmented Generation**
2605.22923v1 by Tom Verhoeff

Large language models can answer questions about textbooks, lecture notes, and programming exercises more reliably when their answers are grounded in an explicit knowledge source. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is a common approach: relevant fragments of a document are retrieved and inserted into the model context before answering. For mathematical and technical material, the original LaTeX source can be a better starting point than a PDF, because it contains structural information, labels, sectioning commands, macros, and authorial intent that are often lost or distorted in PDF extraction. However, LaTeX source is not automatically AI-friendly. Cross-references must be resolved, custom macros must be interpreted, exercises and examples must be identified, and author-supplied semantic metadata may be needed. This article describes a focused preprocessing approach for turning LaTeX source, together with its compiled auxiliary files and optional author annotations, into Markdown and JSONL chunks suitable for indexing in a vector database.

摘要：大型語言模型在回答有關教科書、講義和程式練習的問題時，當其答案基於明確的知識來源時，能夠更可靠地提供回應。檢索增強生成（RAG）是一種常見的方法：相關的文檔片段會被檢索並插入到模型的上下文中，然後再進行回答。對於數學和技術材料而言，原始的 LaTeX 源碼可能比 PDF 更適合作為起點，因為它包含了結構信息、標籤、分段命令、宏和作者意圖，而這些在 PDF 提取中往往會丟失或扭曲。然而，LaTeX 源碼並不是自動對 AI 友好的。交叉引用必須被解決，自定義宏必須被解釋，練習和例子必須被識別，並且可能需要作者提供的語義元數據。本文描述了一種專注的預處理方法，用於將 LaTeX 源碼及其編譯的輔助文件和可選的作者註釋轉換為適合在向量數據庫中索引的 Markdown 和 JSONL 區塊。

##### **MOSS: Self-Evolution through Source-Level Rewriting in Autonomous Agent Systems**
2605.22794v1 by Qianshu Cai, Yonggang Zhang, Xianzhang Jia, Wei Xue, Jun Song, Xinmei Tian, Yike Guo

Autonomous agentic systems are largely static after deployment: they do not learn from user interactions, and recurring failures persist until the next human-driven update ships a fix. Self-evolving agents have emerged in response, but all confine evolution to text-mutable artifacts -- skill files, prompt configurations, memory schemas, workflow graphs -- and leave the agent harness untouched. Since routing, hook ordering, state invariants, and dispatch live in code rather than in any text artifact, an entire class of structural failure is physically unreachable from the text layer. We argue that source-level adaptation is a fundamentally more general medium: it is Turing-complete, a strict superset of every text-mutable scope, takes effect deterministically rather than through base-model compliance, and does not erode under long-context drift. We present MOSS, a system that performs self-rewriting at the source level on production agentic substrates. Each evolution is anchored to an automatically curated batch of production-failure evidence and proceeds through a deterministic multi-stage pipeline; code modification is delegated to a pluggable external coding-agent CLI while MOSS retains stage ordering and verdicts. Candidates are verified by replaying the batch against the candidate image in ephemeral trial workers, then promoted via user-consent-gated, in-place container swap with health-probe-gated rollback. On OpenClaw, MOSS lifts a four-task mean grader score from 0.25 to 0.61 in a single cycle without human intervention.

摘要：自主代理系統在部署後基本上是靜態的：它們不會從用戶互動中學習，且重複的失敗會持續存在，直到下一次人為驅動的更新發佈修復。自我進化的代理隨之出現，但所有的進化都限於文本可變的工件——技能檔案、提示配置、記憶架構、工作流程圖——並且不觸及代理的框架。由於路由、掛鉤順序、狀態不變量和調度都存在於代碼中，而不是任何文本工件中，整個結構性失敗類別在文本層面上是物理上無法到達的。我們主張源級適應是一種根本上更通用的媒介：它是圖靈完備的，是每個文本可變範疇的嚴格超集，具有確定性效果，而不是通過基礎模型的合規性來實現，並且在長期上下文漂移下不會退化。我們提出了MOSS，一個在生產代理基底上進行源級自我重寫的系統。每次進化都依賴於自動策劃的生產失敗證據批次，並通過確定性的多階段管道進行；代碼修改委託給可插拔的外部編碼代理CLI，而MOSS保留階段順序和裁決。候選者通過在短暫的試驗工作者中重放批次以驗證候選映像，然後通過用戶同意的就地容器交換進行提升，並進行健康探測的回滾。在OpenClaw上，MOSS在單個周期內將四任務平均評分從0.25提升到0.61，無需人為干預。

##### **Transcoders Trace Visual Grounding and Hallucinations in Vision-Language Models**
2605.22902v1 by Dimitrios Damianos, Leon Voukoutis, Georgios Skyrianos, Vassilis Katsouros, Georgios Paraskevopoulos

Generative Vision-Language Models (VLMs) perform well on multimodal reasoning, but how visual inputs are transformed to text remains poorly understood. Existing interpretability work on VLMs uses Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs), which decompose static residual representations and miss the functional updates that drive cross-modal interaction. We adopt a function-centric framework based on Transcoders, sparse approximations of MLP sublayers that act as a causal proxy for layer-wise computation. Applied to Gemma 3-4B-IT, the framework decomposes the model into interpretable computational pathways linking image patches to directions in token generation. Transcoder attributions produce stronger and more stable effects on visually grounded tokens under patch ablation than SAE attributions, and align better with semantically relevant image regions. A False Visual Grounding counterfactual analysis confirms that the recovered pathways are specific to vision-language interaction.Finally, we perform a structural analysis of hallucinated generations, by extracting graph-based indicators from circuit traces produced by the transcoders. A logistic classifier over these mechanistic graph features predicts hallucinations at AUC $0.68$. These results show that function-centric circuit decomposition yields interpretable and predictive accounts of multimodal computation in VLMs.

摘要：生成式視覺-語言模型（VLMs）在多模態推理上表現良好，但視覺輸入如何轉換為文本仍然不甚了解。現有對VLMs的可解釋性研究使用稀疏自編碼器（SAEs），這些自編碼器分解靜態殘差表示，卻忽略了驅動跨模態互動的功能性更新。我們採用一個基於轉碼器的功能中心框架，轉碼器是MLP子層的稀疏近似，作為層級計算的因果代理。應用於Gemma 3-4B-IT，該框架將模型分解為可解釋的計算路徑，將圖像區塊與標記生成中的方向鏈接起來。在區塊消融下，轉碼器的歸因對視覺基礎標記產生了比SAE歸因更強且更穩定的效果，並且與語義相關的圖像區域對齊得更好。一項虛假視覺基礎的反事實分析確認，恢復的路徑是特定於視覺-語言互動的。最後，我們通過從轉碼器產生的電路跡象中提取基於圖形的指標，對幻覺生成進行結構分析。對這些機械圖形特徵的邏輯回歸分類器預測幻覺的AUC為$0.68$。這些結果顯示，功能中心的電路分解提供了對VLMs中多模態計算的可解釋和可預測的解釋。

##### **Understanding Data Temporality Impact on Large Language Models Pre-training**
2605.22769v1 by Pilchen Hippolyte, Fabre Romain, Signe Talla Franck, Perez Patrick, Grave Edouard

Large language models (LLMs) are typically trained on shuffled corpora, yielding models whose knowledge is frozen at train time and whose temporal grounding remains poorly understood. In this work, we study the impact of pre-training dynamics on the acquisition of time-sensitive factual knowledge, focusing specifically on data ordering. Our main contributions are twofold. First, we introduce a comprehensive benchmark of over 7,000 temporally grounded questions and an evaluation protocol that enables analysis of whether models correctly associate facts with their corresponding time periods. Second, we pretrain 6B-parameter models on temporally ordered Common Crawl snapshots and compare them against standard shuffled pre-training. Our results show that sequentially trained models match shuffled baselines on general language understanding and common knowledge while consistently exhibiting more up-to-date and temporally precise knowledge. Temporally ordered pre-training yields improved factual freshness, while shuffled pre-training peaks on older data, possibly due to increased factual repetition. These findings, along with the release of our code at https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos , checkpoints, and datasets at https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos provide a foundation for future research on continual learning for LLMs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）通常在隨機排列的語料庫上進行訓練，產生的模型其知識在訓練時被凍結，且其時間基礎仍然不甚了解。<lb/>在本研究中，我們探討了預訓練動態對於獲取時間敏感事實知識的影響，特別關注數據排序。<lb/>我們的主要貢獻有兩個方面。<lb/>首先，我們引入了一個包含超過7,000個時間基礎問題的綜合基準，以及一個評估協議，使得可以分析模型是否正確將事實與其對應的時間段關聯起來。<lb/>其次，我們在時間排序的Common Crawl快照上預訓練了6B參數模型，並將其與標準的隨機預訓練進行比較。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，按順序訓練的模型在一般語言理解和常識上與隨機基準相匹配，同時持續展現出更為最新和時間上精確的知識。<lb/>時間排序的預訓練提高了事實的新鮮度，而隨機預訓練則在舊數據上達到高峰，這可能是由於事實重複的增加。<lb/>這些發現，以及我們的代碼在 https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos 、檢查點和數據集在 https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos 的發布，為未來對LLMs的持續學習研究提供了基礎。

##### **Advancing Mathematics Research with AI-Driven Formal Proof Search**
2605.22763v1 by George Tsoukalas, Anton Kovsharov, Sergey Shirobokov, Anja Surina, Moritz Firsching, Gergely Bérczi, Francisco J. R. Ruiz, Arun Suggala, Adam Zsolt Wagner, Eric Wieser, Lei Yu, Aja Huang, Miklós Z. Horváth, Andrew Ferrauiolo, Henryk Michalewski, Codrut Grosu, Thomas Hubert, Matej Balog, Pushmeet Kohli, Swarat Chaudhuri

Large language models (LLMs) increasingly excel at mathematical reasoning, but their unreliability limits their utility in mathematics research. A mitigation is using LLMs to generate formal proofs in languages like Lean. We perform the first large-scale evaluation of this method's ability to solve open problems. Our most capable agent autonomously resolved 9 of 353 open Erdős problems at the per-problem cost of a few hundred dollars, proved 44/492 OEIS conjectures, and is being deployed in combinatorics, optimization, graph theory, algebraic geometry, and quantum optics research. A basic agent alternating LLM-based generation with Lean-based verification replicated the Erdős successes but proved costlier on the hardest problems. These findings demonstrate the power of AI-aided formal proof search and shed light on the agent designs that enable it.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在數學推理方面越來越出色，但它們的不可靠性限制了它們在數學研究中的實用性。一種緩解方法是使用LLMs生成像Lean這樣的語言中的正式證明。我們對這種方法解決未解決問題的能力進行了首次大規模評估。我們最強大的代理自主解決了353個開放的Erdős問題中的9個，每個問題的成本為幾百美元，證明了44/492個OEIS猜想，並正在應用於組合學、優化、圖論、代數幾何和量子光學研究。一個基本的代理交替使用基於LLM的生成和基於Lean的驗證，複製了Erdős的成功，但在最難的問題上成本更高。這些發現展示了AI輔助正式證明搜索的力量，並闡明了使其可行的代理設計。

##### **ChronoMedKG: A Temporally-Grounded Biomedical Knowledge Graph and Benchmark for Clinical Reasoning**
2605.22734v1 by Md Shamim Ahmed, Farzaneh Firoozbakht, Lukas Galke Poech, Jan Baumbach, Richard Röttger

Biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) treat disease associations as static facts, but temporal information is crucial for clinical reasoning, e.g., a symptom diagnostic of one disease at age 3 may imply a different disease at age 13. Existing KGs such as PrimeKG, Hetionet, and iKraph do not encode when a finding becomes clinically relevant over the course of a disease. This limits their usefulness for longitudinal clinical reasoning and retrieval augmentation.
  We introduce ChronoMedKG, a temporal biomedical knowledge graph that contains 460,497 evidence-linked triples (filtered from 13M raw extractions) covering 13,431 diseases. Each association is tied to temporal components like onset window or progression stage, which are backed by PMID-traceable evidence and a multi-signal credibility score. The graph is constructed through a disease-autonomous multi-agent pipeline in which multiple frontier LLMs independently extract knowledge from PubMed and PMC literature. Only those relations are kept that are supported by multi-model consensus, survive credibility filtering, as well as ontology alignment.
  ChronoMedKG scored 92.7% agreement against Orphadata and adds temporal grounding for 6,250 diseases absent from HPOA, Orphadata, and Phenopackets, including 1,657 Orphanet-coded rare diseases. We further introduce ChronoTQA, a benchmark of 3,341 questions across eight task types (six temporal plus two static controls), with a 12-question supplementary probe. Frontier LLMs lose roughly 30 points moving from static to temporal questions; ChronoMedKG retrieval rescues 47-65% of their long-tail failures, against 17-29% for HPOA-RAG. As such, ChronoMedKG provides a crucial temporal axis for retrieval-augmented clinical systems that was previously absent.

摘要：生物醫學知識圖譜（KGs）將疾病關聯視為靜態事實，但時間信息對於臨床推理至關重要，例如，3歲時診斷為某種疾病的症狀可能在13歲時暗示另一種疾病。現有的KGs，如PrimeKG、Hetionet和iKraph，並未編碼在疾病過程中何時發現變得臨床相關。這限制了它們在縱向臨床推理和檢索增強方面的實用性。<lb/>
我們介紹ChronoMedKG，一個包含460,497個證據鏈接三元組的時間生物醫學知識圖譜（從1300萬個原始提取中過濾而來），涵蓋13,431種疾病。每個關聯都與時間組件相關，如發病窗口或進展階段，這些都由PMID可追溯的證據和多信號可信度分數支持。該圖譜是通過一個疾病自主的多代理管道構建的，其中多個前沿LLMs獨立從PubMed和PMC文獻中提取知識。僅保留那些得到多模型共識支持、經過可信度過濾以及本體對齊的關係。<lb/>
ChronoMedKG在Orphadata上得分92.7%的一致性，並為6,250種在HPOA、Orphadata和Phenopackets中缺失的疾病提供了時間基礎，包括1,657種Orphanet編碼的罕見疾病。我們進一步介紹ChronoTQA，一個涵蓋八種任務類型（六種時間性加兩種靜態控制）的3,341個問題基準，並附有12個問題的補充探測。前沿LLMs在靜態問題轉向時間性問題時大約損失30分；ChronoMedKG檢索挽救了47-65%的長尾失敗，而HPOA-RAG則為17-29%。因此，ChronoMedKG為增強檢索的臨床系統提供了一個至關重要的時間軸，這在之前是缺失的。

##### **AnyMo: Geometry-Aware Setup-Agnostic Modeling of Human Motion in the Wild**
2605.22715v1 by Baiyu Chen, Zechen Li, Wilson Wongso, Lihuan Li, Xiachong Lin, Hao Xue, Benjamin Tag, Flora Salim

As wearable and mobile devices become increasingly embedded in daily life, they offer a practical way to continuously sense human motion in the wild. But inertial signals are highly dependent on the sensing setup, including body location, mounting position, sensor orientation, device hardware, and sampling protocol. This setup dependence makes it difficult to learn motion representations that transfer across devices and datasets, and limits the broader use of wearable IMUs beyond closed-set recognition. We introduce AnyMo, a geometry-aware framework for setup-agnostic human motion modeling. AnyMo uses physics-grounded IMU simulation over dense body-surface placements to generate diverse and plausible synthetic signals, pre-trains a graph encoder from paired synthetic placement views and masked partial observations, tokenizes multi-position IMU into full-body motion tokens, and aligns these tokens with an LLM for motion-language understanding. We evaluate AnyMo on three complementary tasks: zero-shot activity recognition across 14 unseen downstream datasets, cross-modal retrieval, and wearable IMU motion captioning, where it improves average Accuracy/F1/R@2 by 11.7\%/11.6\%/22.6\% on HAR, increases zero-shot IMU-to-text and text-to-IMU retrieval MRR by 15.9\% and 28.6\%, respectively, and improves zero-shot captioning BERT-F1 by 18.8\%. These results support AnyMo as a generalist model for wearable motion understanding in the wild. Project page: https://baiyuchen.com/project/AnyMo.

摘要：隨著可穿戴和移動設備越來越深入日常生活，它們提供了一種實用的方法來持續感知人類在自然環境中的運動。<lb/>但是，慣性信號高度依賴於感測設置，包括身體位置、安裝位置、感測器方向、設備硬體和取樣協議。<lb/>這種設置依賴性使得學習能夠跨設備和數據集轉移的運動表示變得困難，並限制了可穿戴IMU在封閉集識別之外的更廣泛應用。<lb/>我們介紹了AnyMo，一個對設置無關的人類運動建模的幾何感知框架。<lb/>AnyMo使用基於物理的IMU模擬，通過密集的身體表面放置來生成多樣且合理的合成信號，從配對的合成放置視圖和遮蔽的部分觀察中預訓練圖編碼器，將多位置IMU標記為全身運動標記，並將這些標記與LLM對齊以實現運動-語言理解。<lb/>我們在三個互補任務上評估AnyMo：在14個未見的下游數據集上進行零樣本活動識別，跨模態檢索，以及可穿戴IMU運動標註，在HAR上平均準確率/F1/R@2提高了11.7\%/11.6\%/22.6\%，零樣本IMU到文本和文本到IMU檢索的MRR分別提高了15.9\%和28.6\%，並且零樣本標註的BERT-F1提高了18.8\%。<lb/>這些結果支持AnyMo作為一個通用模型，用於在自然環境中理解可穿戴運動。<lb/>項目頁面：https://baiyuchen.com/project/AnyMo。

##### **Scout-Assisted Planning for Heterogeneous Robot Teams under Partially Known Environments**
2605.22693v1 by Hoang-Dung Bui, Abhish Khanal, Raihan Islam Arnob, Gregory J. Stein

Autonomous robot teams navigating partially known environments face costly backtracking when ground robots encounter blocked roads that are only revealed upon physical traversal. We address this with Scout-Assisted Planning, a heterogeneous planning framework in which scouting Unmanned Aerial Vehicles proactively gather environmental information to improve Unmanned Ground Vehicle navigation. To focus scouting on the most consequential edges, we propose Information Gain-based Action Pruning, which scores candidate scouting actions by their expected impact on ground robot behavior. Since exact Information Gain-based Action Pruning computation is prohibitively expensive, we develop a Graph Neural Network based model that predicts information gain values directly from graph structure and belief state, reducing planning time to real-time levels without sacrificing solution quality. Experiments across three environment types show that SAP with Information Gain Action Pruning reduces ground robot travel cost by 31.9--37.7% over the Canadian Traveler Problem baseline, and outperforms proximity-based scouting guidance by an additional 8--14%, confirming that principled information-gain-guided scouting is both more effective and computationally feasible for real-world deployment

摘要：自主機器人團隊在部分已知環境中導航時，當地面機器人遇到被封鎖的道路時，會面臨昂貴的回溯成本，這些封鎖的道路只有在實際通行後才能揭示。我們通過偵查輔助規劃來解決這一問題，這是一種異質規劃框架，其中偵查無人機主動收集環境信息，以改善無人地面車輛的導航。為了將偵查集中在最重要的邊緣上，我們提出了基於信息增益的行動修剪，通過預期對地面機器人行為的影響來評分候選偵查行動。由於精確的基於信息增益的行動修剪計算成本過高，我們開發了一種基於圖神經網絡的模型，該模型直接從圖結構和信念狀態預測信息增益值，將規劃時間減少到實時水平而不犧牲解決方案質量。三種環境類型的實驗顯示，使用基於信息增益的行動修剪的SAP比加拿大旅行者問題基線降低了31.9%到37.7%的地面機器人旅行成本，並且比基於接近度的偵查指導額外提高了8%到14%的性能，證實了有原則的信息增益指導的偵查在現實世界部署中既更有效又計算上可行。

##### **Forecasting Scientific Progress with Artificial Intelligence**
2605.22681v1 by Sean Wu, Pan Lu, Yupeng Chen, Jonathan Bragg, Yutaro Yamada, Peter Clark, David Clifton, Philip Torr, James Zou, Junchi Yu

Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly embedded in scientific discovery, yet whether it can anticipate scientific progress remains unclear. To study this question, we introduce a temporally grounded evaluation framework for forecasting scientific progress under controlled knowledge constraints. We present CUSP (Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress), a multi-disciplinary and event-level benchmark that evaluates scientific forecasting in AI systems through feasibility assessment, mechanistic reasoning, generative solution design, and temporal prediction. Across 4,760 scientific events, we observe systematic and domain-dependent limitations in current frontier models. While models can identify plausible research directions from competing candidates, they fail to reliably predict whether scientific advances will be realized and systematically misestimate when they will occur. Performance is highly heterogeneous across domains, with the timing of AI progress more predictable than advances in biology, chemistry, and physics. Performance is largely insensitive to whether events occur before or after the training cutoff, suggesting these limitations cannot be explained solely by knowledge exposure in training data. Under controlled information access, additional pre-cutoff knowledge improves performance but does not close the gap to full-information settings, which becomes more pronounced for high-citation advances. Models also exhibit systematic overconfidence and strong response biases, indicating unreliable uncertainty estimation. Taken together, current AI systems fall short as predictive tools for scientific progress. Access to prior knowledge does not translate into reliable forecasting, and performance benefits more from post-event information than from forward-looking prediction.

摘要：人工智慧（AI）越來越多地嵌入科學發現中，但它是否能預測科學進展仍不清楚。為了研究這個問題，我們引入了一個基於時間的評估框架，用於在受控知識約束下預測科學進展。我們提出了 CUSP（Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress），這是一個跨學科的事件級基準，通過可行性評估、機制推理、生成解決方案設計和時間預測來評估 AI 系統中的科學預測。在 4,760 個科學事件中，我們觀察到當前前沿模型存在系統性和領域依賴的限制。儘管模型可以從競爭候選者中識別出合理的研究方向，但它們無法可靠地預測科學進展是否會實現，並且系統性地錯誤估計其發生時間。不同領域的表現差異很大，AI 進展的時間預測比生物學、化學和物理學的進展更具可預測性。表現在事件發生在訓練截止之前或之後的情況下大體上不敏感，這表明這些限制不能僅僅通過訓練數據中的知識曝光來解釋。在受控信息訪問下，額外的截止前知識提高了表現，但並未縮小與全信息設置之間的差距，這在高引用的進展中變得更加明顯。模型還表現出系統性的過度自信和強烈的反應偏見，顯示出不可靠的不確定性估計。綜合來看，當前的 AI 系統作為預測科學進展的工具仍然不足。獲取先前的知識並未轉化為可靠的預測，並且表現更受事件後信息的影響，而不是來自前瞻性的預測。

##### **Is Capability a Liability? More Capable Language Models Make Worse Forecasts When It Matters Most**
2605.22672v2 by Nick Merrill, Jaeho Lee, Ezra Karger

We document inverse scaling in LLMs on forecasting problems whose underlying time series exhibit superlinear growth and tail risk of regime change, a structure common in finance and epidemiology. On these tasks, more capable models produce worse distributional forecasts. The pattern appears on ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim), a contamination-free, simulated-world benchmark we release, in forecasting synthetic SIR epidemics with a matched linear control, and replicates in real-world datasets on COVID-19, measles, housing markets, and hyperinflation. A per-quantile decomposition shows the failure concentrates at the upper tail, which more capable models shift upward to track aggressive extrapolations of growth, while the lower tail stays put. A within-family study of Llama-3.1 shows that both model scale and post-training independently contribute to this effect. Domain knowledge does not reliably rescue calibration. This inverse scaling does not appear on single-threshold metrics common in LLM forecasting benchmarks, reversing the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on identical outputs. Single-threshold scoring at conventional cutoffs misses the upper-tail cost; tail-inclusive scoring reverses the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on the same outputs. We recommend that LLM forecasting evaluations use continuous (and unbounded) measures of accuracy alongside bounded binary threshold metrics.

摘要：我們記錄了在預測問題中大型語言模型（LLMs）的逆縮放，這些問題的基礎時間序列展示了超線性增長和制度變化的尾部風險，這種結構在金融和流行病學中很常見。在這些任務中，更強大的模型產生了更差的分佈預測。這一模式出現在我們發布的無污染模擬世界基準ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim)中，預測合成的SIR流行病，並配有匹配的線性控制，並在COVID-19、麻疹、房地產市場和惡性通貨膨脹的現實數據集中重現。每個分位數的分解顯示，失敗集中在上尾，更強大的模型將其向上移動以追蹤增長的激進外推，而下尾則保持不變。對Llama-3.1的家庭內研究顯示，模型規模和訓練後的影響獨立地對這一效應作出貢獻。領域知識並不能可靠地改善校準。這種逆縮放在LLM預測基準中常見的單閾值指標上並不明顯，反轉了相同輸出中能力與準確性之間的關係符號。在傳統的截止點進行單閾值評分時，未能考慮上尾成本；包含尾部的評分則反轉了相同輸出中能力與準確性之間的關係符號。我們建議LLM預測評估使用連續（且無界限）的準確性測量，並與有界的二元閾值指標一起使用。

##### **More Context, Larger Models, or Moral Knowledge? A Systematic Study of Schwartz Value Detection in Political Texts**
2605.22641v2 by Víctor Yeste, Paolo Rosso

Detecting Schwartz values in political text is difficult because implicit cues often depend on surrounding arguments and fine-grained distinctions between neighboring values. We study when context and explicit moral knowledge help sentence-level value detection. Using the ValuesML/Touché ValueEval format, we compare sentence, window, and full-document inputs; no-RAG and retrieval-augmented settings with a curated moral knowledge base; supervised DeBERTa-v3-base/large encoders; and zero-shot LLMs from 12B to 123B parameters. The results show that more context is not uniformly better: full-document context improves supervised DeBERTa encoders by 3.8-4.8 macro-F1 points over sentence-only input, but does not consistently help zero-shot LLMs. Retrieved moral knowledge is more consistently useful in matched comparisons, improving each tested model family and context condition under early fusion. However, scaling from DeBERTa-v3-base to large and from 12B to larger LLMs does not guarantee gains, and simple early fusion outperforms the tested late-fusion and cross-attention RAG variants for encoders. Per-value analyses show that context and retrieval help most for socially situated or conceptually confusable values. These findings suggest that value-sensitive NLP should evaluate context, knowledge, and model family jointly rather than treating longer inputs or larger models as universal improvements.

摘要：在政治文本中檢測施瓦茨值是困難的，因為隱含的線索往往依賴於周圍的論點以及相鄰值之間的細微區別。<lb/>我們研究了何時上下文和明確的道德知識有助於句子層級的價值檢測。<lb/>使用ValuesML/Touché ValueEval格式，我們比較了句子、窗口和完整文檔輸入；無RAG和增強檢索的設置，並使用經過策劃的道德知識庫；監督式DeBERTa-v3-base/large編碼器；以及從12B到123B參數的零-shot LLM。<lb/>結果顯示，更多的上下文並不總是更好：完整文檔上下文使監督式DeBERTa編碼器的表現提高了3.8-4.8的宏F1分數，相較於僅使用句子輸入，但對零-shot LLM並不總是有幫助。<lb/>檢索到的道德知識在匹配比較中更為一致地有用，改善了每個測試的模型家族和上下文條件，尤其是在早期融合下。<lb/>然而，從DeBERTa-v3-base擴展到large，以及從12B擴展到更大的LLM並不保證會有增益，並且簡單的早期融合在編碼器中表現優於測試的晚期融合和交叉注意RAG變體。<lb/>逐值分析顯示，上下文和檢索對社會情境或概念上混淆的值幫助最大。<lb/>這些發現表明，價值敏感的NLP應該聯合評估上下文、知識和模型家族，而不是將更長的輸入或更大的模型視為普遍的改進。

##### **Chinese sensorimotor and embodiment norms for 3,000 lexicalized concepts**
2605.22616v1 by Jing Chen, Gábor Parti, Yin Zhong, Chu-Ren Huang, Marco Marelli

Understanding how conceptual knowledge is grounded in bodily experience, and to what extent machine systems can acquire such knowledge without direct sensorimotor experience, are central questions in both cognitive science and embodied artificial intelligence research. Large-scale normative resources are essential for investigating these questions empirically, yet such resources remain sparse for non-Indo-European languages. We present a novel normative database for 3,000 lexicalized concepts in Mandarin Chinese, comprising 11-dimensional sensorimotor ratings and unidimensional embodiment ratings collected from 378 native Mandarin speakers. The ratings demonstrate high reliability and strong cross-norm validity with existing Chinese resources, each of which covers fewer words and a subset of the 11 sensorimotor dimensions. In a validation study, we tested new variables derived from a theoretically motivated metric, Perceptual Strength of Embodiment (PSE) (Huang et al., 2025), together with seven common composite variables, on lexical decision tasks. The results suggest that PSE-Sensorimotor and Minkowski-3 are the strongest composite predictors of lexical decision performance, capturing the facilitatory effects of sensorimotor information on lexical processing. A further exploratory study showed that sensorimotor ratings are substantially recoverable from purely linguistic representations using simple regression models (mean Spearman r = .62 across dimensions), though recovery varied markedly: visual and auditory dimensions yielded higher correspondence than chemosensory ones. Representational similarity analysis further showed that the relational geometry of the sensorimotor space is also partially recoverable (r = .540), consistent with the view that distributional language use encodes aspects of embodied conceptual structure.

摘要：理解概念知識如何根植於身體經驗，以及機器系統在多大程度上可以獲得這種知識而無需直接的感覺運動經驗，是認知科學和具身人工智慧研究中的核心問題。大規模的規範資源對於實證調查這些問題至關重要，但對於非印歐語言而言，此類資源仍然稀缺。我們提出了一個新穎的規範數據庫，涵蓋了3000個在普通話中的詞彙化概念，包括從378位母語普通話說話者收集的11維感覺運動評分和一維具身評分。這些評分顯示出高可靠性，並與現有的中文資源具有強大的交叉規範有效性，後者每個涵蓋的詞彙數量較少，且僅包含11個感覺運動維度的子集。在一項驗證研究中，我們測試了從理論上動機的度量——具身感知強度（PSE）（Huang et al., 2025）衍生的新變量，以及七個常見的綜合變量，應用於詞彙決策任務。結果表明，PSE-感覺運動和Minkowski-3是詞彙決策表現的最強綜合預測因子，捕捉了感覺運動信息對詞彙處理的促進效應。進一步的探索性研究顯示，感覺運動評分可以從純語言表徵中通過簡單的回歸模型顯著恢復（各維度的平均Spearman r = .62），儘管恢復程度差異顯著：視覺和聽覺維度的對應性高於化學感官維度。表徵相似性分析進一步顯示，感覺運動空間的關係幾何也部分可恢復（r = .540），這與分佈式語言使用編碼具身概念結構某些方面的觀點一致。

##### **Think Thrice Before You Speak: Dual knowledge-enhanced Theory-of-Mind Reasoning for Persuasive Agents**
2605.22602v1 by Minghui Ma, Bin Guo, Runze Yang, Mengqi Chen, Yan Liu, Jingqi Liu, Yahan Pei, Xuehao Ma, Qiuyun Zhang, Zhiwen Yu

Persuasive dialogue requires reasoning about others' latent mental states, a capability known as Theory of Mind (ToM). However, due to reliance on simple prompting strategies and insufficient ToM knowledge, existing LLMs often fail to capture the intrinsic dependencies among mental states, leading to fragmented representations and unstable reasoning. To address these challenges, we introduce the ToM-based Persuasive Dialogue (ToM-PD) task, grounded in the Belief-Desire-Intention (BDI) framework, which explicitly models the sequential dependencies among mental states in multi-turn dialogues. To facilitate research on this task, we construct a large-scale annotated dataset, ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues (ToM-BPD), capturing fine-grained mental states and corresponding persuasive strategies. We further propose Think Thrice Before You Speak (TTBYS), a knowledge-enhanced stepwise reasoning framework that leverages both explicit and implicit prior experiences to improve LLMs' inference of desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that Qwen3-8B equipped with TTBYS outperforms GPT-5 by 1.20%, 22.80%, and 16.97% in predicting desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies, respectively. Case studies further show that our approach enhances interpretability and consistency in reasoning.

摘要：說服性對話需要對他人潛在心理狀態進行推理，這一能力被稱為心智理論（Theory of Mind, ToM）。然而，由於依賴簡單的提示策略和不足的心智理論知識，現有的LLM往往無法捕捉心理狀態之間的內在依賴性，導致片段化的表徵和不穩定的推理。為了解決這些挑戰，我們引入了基於心智理論的說服性對話（ToM-PD）任務，該任務基於信念-欲望-意圖（Belief-Desire-Intention, BDI）框架，明確建模多輪對話中心理狀態之間的序列依賴性。為了促進對這一任務的研究，我們構建了一個大規模的標註數據集，基於心智理論的廣泛說服對話（ToM-BPD），捕捉細緻的心理狀態和相應的說服策略。我們進一步提出了在發言前三思（Think Thrice Before You Speak, TTBYS），這是一個增強知識的逐步推理框架，利用明確和隱含的先前經驗來改善LLM對欲望、信念和說服策略的推斷。實驗結果顯示，配備TTBYS的Qwen3-8B在預測欲望、信念和說服策略方面，分別比GPT-5高出1.20%、22.80%和16.97%。案例研究進一步表明，我們的方法增強了推理的可解釋性和一致性。

##### **Case-Aware Medical Image Classification with Multimodal Knowledge Graphs and Reliability-Guided Refinement**
2605.22547v1 by Yiming Xu, Yixuan Liu, Yuhang Zhang, Ling Zheng, Yihan Wang, Qi Song

Deep learning has brought significant progress to medical image classification, yet most existing methods still rely on isolated visual evidence and cannot effectively leverage similar cases or external knowledge. In clinical practice, diagnosis is typically supported by historical similar cases and their associated symptoms. To simulate this diagnostic process, we propose a framework that performs case-aware reasoning using multimodal knowledge graphs for explainable medical image diagnosis. Given an input image, our method constructs a multimodal knowledge graph from adaptively retrieved similar cases, enabling more effective utilization of related samples. We further introduce a knowledge propagation and injection mechanism, where an image-centric Graph Attention Network propagates knowledge semantics to obtain case-based features, followed by a bidirectional cross-modal attention mechanism that injects these features into visual representations for cross-modal alignment. To mitigate noisy retrieval, we design a confidence-calibrated decision refinement scheme that estimates the reliability of each retrieved case by jointly considering prediction confidence and sample similarity, adaptively adjusting its contribution to the final prediction and providing interpretable case-level evidence. Extensive experiments on multiple medical imaging datasets show that our approach consistently outperforms strong baselines, and ablation studies validate the effectiveness of each component. The source code is publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/MKG-CARE-8B7B.

摘要：深度學習為醫學影像分類帶來了顯著的進展，然而大多數現有方法仍然依賴孤立的視覺證據，無法有效利用相似案例或外部知識。<lb/>在臨床實踐中，診斷通常是由歷史相似案例及其相關症狀所支持。<lb/>為了模擬這一診斷過程，我們提出了一個框架，使用多模態知識圖進行案例感知推理，以實現可解釋的醫學影像診斷。<lb/>給定一個輸入影像，我們的方法從自適應檢索的相似案例中構建多模態知識圖，使相關樣本的利用更加有效。<lb/>我們進一步引入了一種知識傳播和注入機制，其中以影像為中心的圖注意力網絡傳播知識語義，以獲取基於案例的特徵，隨後通過雙向跨模態注意力機制將這些特徵注入視覺表示中，以實現跨模態對齊。<lb/>為了減少噪聲檢索，我們設計了一種信心校準的決策精煉方案，通過共同考慮預測信心和樣本相似性來估計每個檢索案例的可靠性，自適應地調整其對最終預測的貢獻，並提供可解釋的案例級證據。<lb/>在多個醫學影像數據集上進行的廣泛實驗顯示，我們的方法始終超越強基準，消融研究驗證了每個組件的有效性。<lb/>源代碼可在 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/MKG-CARE-8B7B 獲得。

##### **Dynamic Hypergraph Representation Learning for Multivariate Time Series without Prior Knowledge**
2605.22540v1 by Marco Gregnanin, Johannes De Smedt, Giorgio Gnecco, Maurizio Parton

Hypergraphs have the capacity to capture higher-dimensional relationships among entities across various domains, making them a subject of growing interest within the research community for understanding the structure and dynamics of complex systems. However, a key challenge is the derivation of hypergraph representations from time series data in situations where the structure of the hypergraph is limited or absent. In this study, we propose a model that constructs a dynamic hypergraph representation for multivariate time series without relying on prior knowledge of the data. This is achieved by applying community detection to the time series and transforming the resulting communities, obtained through an attention mechanism, into a hypergraph using a clique-based technique. Hypergraph representations are derived from different time series datasets, and the resulting hypergraphs are then used by a Dynamic Hypergraph Attention Convolution Network (DHACN) for multivariate time series predictions. This research advances the field of hypergraph representation by introducing a novel approach that is better suited to uncover high-order relationships without prior knowledge.

摘要：超圖具有捕捉各個領域實體之間高維關係的能力，使其在研究社群中對理解複雜系統的結構和動態變得越來越受到關注。然而，一個主要挑戰是在超圖結構有限或缺失的情況下，從時間序列數據中推導出超圖表示。在本研究中，我們提出了一個模型，該模型為多變量時間序列構建動態超圖表示，而不依賴於對數據的先驗知識。這是通過對時間序列應用社群檢測，並利用注意力機制將所得到的社群轉換為超圖，使用基於團的技術來實現的。超圖表示是從不同的時間序列數據集推導而來，然後由動態超圖注意力卷積網絡（DHACN）用於多變量時間序列預測。本研究通過引入一種更適合於揭示高階關係的新方法，推進了超圖表示的領域，而無需先驗知識。

##### **LACO: Adaptive Latent Communication for Collaborative Driving**
2605.22504v1 by Tianhao Chen, Yuheng Wu, Dongman Lee

Collaborative driving aims to improve safety and efficiency by enabling connected vehicles to coordinate under partial observability. Recent approaches have evolved from sharing visual features for perception to exchanging language-based reasoning through foundation models for behavioral coordination. Though communicating in language provides intuitive information, it introduces two challenges: high latency caused by autoregressive decoding and information loss caused by compressing rich internal representations into discrete tokens. To address these challenges, we analyze latent communication in collaborative driving under inherent limitations of multi-agent settings. Our analysis reveals agent identity confusion, where direct fusion of latent states entangles decision representations across vehicles. Motivated by this, we propose LACO, a training-free \textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication paradigm that seamlessly adapts pretrained driving models to collaborative settings. LACO introduces Iterative Latent Deliberation (ILD) for latent reasoning, Cross-Horizon Saliency Attribution (CHSA) for communication-efficient information selection, and Structured Semantic Knowledge Distillation (SSKD) to stabilize ego-centric decision making. Closed-loop experiments in CARLA show that LACO notably reduces communication and inference latency while maintaining strong collaborative driving performance.

摘要：協作駕駛旨在透過使連接的車輛在部分可觀察性下協調來提高安全性和效率。最近的方法已經從共享視覺特徵以進行感知演變為通過基礎模型進行基於語言的推理交換，以實現行為協調。雖然用語言進行溝通提供了直觀的信息，但它引入了兩個挑戰：由自回歸解碼引起的高延遲和由於將豐富的內部表示壓縮為離散標記而導致的信息損失。為了解決這些挑戰，我們分析了在多代理設置的固有限制下協作駕駛中的潛在通信。我們的分析揭示了代理身份混淆，其中潛在狀態的直接融合使車輛之間的決策表示交纏在一起。受到此啟發，我們提出了LACO，一種無需訓練的\textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication範式，能夠無縫地將預訓練的駕駛模型適應於協作環境。LACO引入了迭代潛在深思（ILD）用於潛在推理，跨地平線顯著性歸因（CHSA）用於通信高效的信息選擇，以及結構化語義知識蒸餾（SSKD）以穩定自我中心的決策。CARLA中的閉環實驗顯示，LACO顯著減少了通信和推理延遲，同時保持強大的協作駕駛性能。

##### **Compiling Agentic Workflows into LLM Weights: Near-Frontier Quality at Two Orders of Magnitude Less Cost**
2605.22502v1 by Simon Dennis, Rivaan Patil, Kevin Shabahang, Hao Guo

Agent orchestration frameworks have proliferated, collectively exceeding 290,000 GitHub stars across LangGraph, CrewAI, Google ADK, OpenAI Agents SDK, Semantic Kernel, Strands, and LlamaIndex. All follow the same pattern: an external orchestrator above the LLM, injecting instructions and routing decisions every turn. Recent work has shown this architecture is dominated for procedural tasks by simply providing the procedure in a frontier model's system prompt [Dennis et al., 2026a], at the cost of consuming the context window, requiring a frontier model for every conversation, and exposing proprietary procedures to third-party providers. Compiling the procedure into the weights of a small fine-tuned model -- creating a subterranean agent -- should resolve all of these concerns, and prior work (SimpleTOD, FireAct, SynTOD, WorkflowLLM, Agent Lumos) has shown the technique works. Yet developer adoption has overwhelmingly favored orchestration. We identify three perceived barriers and address each empirically across travel booking (14 nodes), Zoom support (14 nodes, product-specific knowledge), and insurance claims (55 nodes, 6 decision hubs).

摘要：代理協調框架已經大量增長，LangGraph、CrewAI、Google ADK、OpenAI Agents SDK、Semantic Kernel、Strands 和 LlamaIndex 的 GitHub 星數總計超過 290,000。所有這些框架都遵循相同的模式：在 LLM 之上有一個外部協調器，每次轉換時注入指令和路由決策。最近的研究顯示，這種架構在程序性任務中占主導地位，只需在前沿模型的系統提示中提供程序 [Dennis et al., 2026a]，但這會消耗上下文窗口，要求每次對話都使用前沿模型，並將專有程序暴露給第三方供應商。將程序編譯進小型微調模型的權重中——創建一個地下代理——應該能解決所有這些問題，而先前的工作（SimpleTOD、FireAct、SynTOD、WorkflowLLM、Agent Lumos）已經顯示這種技術是有效的。然而，開發者的採用卻壓倒性地偏向於協調。我們識別了三個感知的障礙，並在旅行訂票（14 個節點）、Zoom 支援（14 個節點，產品特定知識）和保險索賠（55 個節點，6 個決策中心）中實證解決每一個問題。

##### **KAPPS: A knowledge-based CPPS Architecture for the Circular Factory**
2605.22457v1 by Etienne Hoffmann, Jan-Felix Klein, Sören Weindel, Max Goebels, Sebastian Behrendt, Daniel Hernández, Ratan Bahadur Thapa, Jürgen Fleischer, Kai Furmans, Steffen Staab

While linear manufacturing relies on homogeneous materials and predefined process sequences, circular manufacturing reintroduces used products with heterogeneous and uncertain conditions. This shift demands manufacturing systems capable of handling variable product states, dynamically reconfigurable processes, and the integration of human and machine knowledge. Conventional manufacturing IT architectures, designed for stable structures and deterministic execution, are unable to meet these requirements, as they cannot adequately represent and manage the uniqueness of individual components at runtime. Following a design science methodology for developing a Cyber Physical Production System for circular manufacturing, we derive 14 requirements from five complementary perspectives. Based on these requirements, we design KAPPS, a knowledge-based architecture that uses an ontology-grounded knowledge graph as a unifying data backbone, combined with a semantic interface layer to enable consistent data and information integration, reasoning, and communication across heterogeneous systems and services, turning the knowledge graph from an integration layer into the factories authoritative write-time state. KAPPS incorporates modules for constraint enforcement and event-driven planning, enabling incremental adaptation of execution plans under uncertainty and human-machine knowledge exchange. The applicability of KAPPS is demonstrated through two implemented use cases: (i) Anomaly detection and learning through knowledge graph mediated services and (ii) runtime constraint enforcement in a modular conveyor system. Subsequently, the architecture is evaluated against the 14 requirements (ed. abstract shortened)

##### **Don't Forget the Critic: Value-Based Data Rehearsal for Multi-Cyclic Continual Reinforcement Learning**
2605.22454v1 by Benjamin Poole, Andrew Quinn, Li Yang, Minwoo Lee

Data rehearsal has emerged as a leading approach for mitigating catastrophic forgetting in Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL). However, existing work remains confined to policy gradient frameworks, regularizing only actors due to the performance degradation incurred by critic regularization. This actor-centric approach overlooks the potential of data rehearsal for value function approximation. Moreover, existing evaluations in CRL rarely consider multi-cyclic environments where task sequences repeat, a critical real-world scenario that exacerbates forgetting and plasticity. We investigate data rehearsal for Deep Q-Networks using Q-value regularization in multi-cyclic settings and propose Qreg+NWLU which introduces two simple modifications: (1) continuous data rehearsal that dynamically collects and updates stored Q-values throughout training, and (2) "No-Wait" regularization that applies immediately rather than after the first task. Together, these modifications yield improvements in learning efficiency, forgetting mitigation, and knowledge transfer over Qreg and conventional CRL methods within value function approximation settings.

摘要：資料重演已成為減輕持續強化學習（CRL）中災難性遺忘的主要方法。然而，現有的研究仍然局限於策略梯度框架，只對演員進行正則化，因為評論員正則化會導致性能下降。這種以演員為中心的方法忽視了資料重演在價值函數近似中的潛力。此外，現有的CRL評估很少考慮多循環環境，其中任務序列重複，這是一個加劇遺忘和可塑性的關鍵現實場景。我們研究了在多循環環境中使用Q值正則化的深度Q網絡資料重演，並提出了Qreg+NWLU，該方法引入了兩個簡單的修改：（1）持續的資料重演，動態收集和更新訓練過程中的儲存Q值，以及（2）“無等待”正則化，立即應用而不是在第一個任務之後。這些修改共同提高了學習效率、減輕遺忘和知識轉移，相比於Qreg和傳統CRL方法在價值函數近似設置中的表現。

##### **Assisted Counterspeech Writing at the Crossroads of Hate Speech and Misinformation**
2605.22435v1 by Genoveffa Martone, Helena Bonaldi, Marco Guerini

Hate speech and misinformation frequently co-occur online, amplifying prejudice and polarization. Given their scale, using Large Language Models (LLMs) to assist expert counterspeech (CS) writing has gained interest, yet prior work has addressed these phenomena separately. We bridge this gap by studying CS generation in contexts where both hate and misinformation co-occur. We test three knowledge-driven generation strategies: first we prompt an LLM with fact-checkers' guidelines and fact-checking articles; secondly, with NGOs' guidelines and reports; thirdly, we create a mixed strategy that combines guidelines and documents from both. 23 experts revise the generated CS, which are assessed via human and automatic metrics. While LLMs produce adequate CS in 40% of cases, expert edits substantially improve naturalness, exhaustiveness, and adherence to guidelines. Based on the post-edited CS, the mixed strategy proves to be the most effective in crowdsourcing evaluation, pairing strong factual correction with stereotype mitigation and empathetic engagement. We release a dataset of hateful and misinformed claims with expert-verified CS and supporting knowledge.

摘要：仇恨言論和錯誤資訊在線上經常同時出現，擴大了偏見和極化。考慮到它們的規模，使用大型語言模型（LLMs）來協助專家反駁言論（CS）寫作引起了興趣，然而之前的研究將這些現象分開處理。我們通過研究在仇恨和錯誤資訊同時出現的情境下的CS生成來填補這一空白。我們測試了三種知識驅動的生成策略：首先，我們用事實查核者的指導方針和事實查核文章來提示LLM；其次，使用非政府組織的指導方針和報告；第三，我們創建了一種混合策略，結合了來自兩者的指導方針和文件。23位專家對生成的CS進行修訂，並通過人類和自動化指標進行評估。雖然LLMs在40%的案例中生成了足夠的CS，但專家的編輯顯著提高了自然性、全面性和對指導方針的遵循。根據後編輯的CS，混合策略在眾包評估中被證明是最有效的，將強有力的事實修正與刻板印象緩解和同理心參與相結合。我們發布了一個包含仇恨和錯誤資訊主張的數據集，並附有專家驗證的CS和支持知識。

##### **Epicure: Navigating the Emergent Geometry of Food Ingredient Embeddings**
2605.22391v1 by Jakub Radzikowski, Josef Chen

We present Epicure, a family of three sibling skip-gram ingredient embeddings retrained from scratch on a multilingual recipe corpus. We aggregate 4.14M recipes from 11 sources spanning seven languages, English, Chinese, Russian, Vietnamese, Spanish, Turkish, Indonesian, German, and Indian-English, and normalise the raw ingredient strings to 1,790 canonical entries via an LLM-augmented pipeline. A 203,508-edge ingredient-ingredient NPMI graph and an 80,019-edge typed FlavorDB ingredient-compound graph, 2,247 typed compound nodes across 15 categories, seed three Metapath2Vec variants that share architecture and hyperparameters and differ only in the random-walk schema: Cooc walks the co-occurrence graph only, Chem walks the typed compound metapaths only, and Core blends both via injected ingredient-ingredient walks at controlled mixing, placing each model at a distinct point on the chemistry-vs-recipe-context spectrum.

摘要：我們介紹 Epicure，一個由三個兄弟姐妹組成的 skip-gram 食材嵌入模型，從頭開始在多語言食譜語料庫上重新訓練。<lb/>我們從 11 個來源聚合了 4.14M 食譜，涵蓋七種語言：英語、中文、俄語、越南語、西班牙語、土耳其語、印尼語、德語和印度英語，並通過 LLM 增強的管道將原始食材字符串標準化為 1,790 個典範條目。<lb/>一個 203,508 邊的食材-食材 NPMI 圖和一個 80,019 邊的類型化 FlavorDB 食材-化合物圖，涵蓋 15 類的 2,247 個類型化化合物節點，為三個 Metapath2Vec 變體提供種子，這些變體共享架構和超參數，僅在隨機漫遊方案上有所不同：Cooc 僅在共現圖上漫遊，Chem 僅在類型化化合物的元路徑上漫遊，而 Core 通過在控制混合下注入的食材-食材漫遊來融合兩者，將每個模型放置在化學與食譜上下文光譜的不同點上。

##### **SepsisAI Orchestrator: A Containerized and Scalable Platform for Deploying AI Models and Real-Time Monitoring in Early Sepsis Detection**
2605.22331v1 by Santiago Ospitia, John Sanabria, John Garcia-Henao

Despite strong predictive results in the clinical machine learning literature, the translation of these models into bedside use remains limited by systems-level barriers: heterogeneous data representations, the absence of standardized deployment workflows, and a mismatch between research prototypes and the concurrency and latency requirements of hospital environments. We present the SepsisAI-Orchestrator, an open-source modular platform that addresses this deployment gap for early sepsis detection. The platform integrates HL7 FHIR-inspired Clinical Document Architecture (CDA) preprocessing, NoSQL storage, a containerized LightGBM classifier served via REST APIs, and a Streamlit clinical dashboard, orchestrated with Docker and Kubernetes. A previously validated LightGBM model (F1 0.87-0.94 on PhysioNet 2019) is reused without modification; the contribution lies in the surrounding infrastructure and its empirical characterization under load. Using k6 with 50-1000 concurrent virtual users, we find that replica count must be matched to the physical CPU thread count of the host: scaling from 3 to 12 replicas on a 12-thread CPU reduces p95 latency from 3.3s to 1.41s (57.3% reduction) and eliminates all request failures, while over-provisioning to 24 or 48 replicas degrades performance due to scheduler contention. To our knowledge this U-shaped scaling behavior has not been quantified previously for clinical AI inference workloads. We do not claim prospective clinical validation. Source code and deployment manifests are available at https://github.com/nucleusai/sepsisai-orchestrator.

摘要：儘管臨床機器學習文獻中有強大的預測結果，但這些模型轉化為臨床應用仍然受到系統層級障礙的限制：異質數據表示、缺乏標準化的部署工作流程，以及研究原型與醫院環境的並發性和延遲要求之間的不匹配。我們提出了SepsisAI-Orchestrator，一個開源的模組化平台，旨在解決早期敗血症檢測的部署差距。該平台整合了受HL7 FHIR啟發的臨床文檔架構（CDA）預處理、NoSQL存儲、通過REST API提供的容器化LightGBM分類器，以及Streamlit臨床儀表板，並使用Docker和Kubernetes進行協調。先前經過驗證的LightGBM模型（在PhysioNet 2019上的F1為0.87-0.94）未經修改地重用；貢獻在於周邊基礎設施及其在負載下的實證特徵。使用k6進行50-1000個並發虛擬用戶的測試，我們發現副本數量必須與主機的物理CPU線程數量相匹配：在12線程CPU上將副本數量從3擴展到12，將p95延遲從3.3秒降低到1.41秒（減少57.3%），並消除了所有請求失敗，而過度配置到24或48個副本則因調度器競爭而降低性能。據我們所知，這種U型擴展行為之前尚未對臨床AI推理工作負載進行量化。我們不聲稱有前瞻性的臨床驗證。源代碼和部署清單可在https://github.com/nucleusai/sepsisai-orchestrator獲得。

##### **Evaluation of Pipelines for Data Integration into Knowledge Graphs**
2605.22304v1 by Marvin Hofer, Erhard Rahm

Integrating new data into knowledge graphs (KG) typically involves different tasks that are executed within workflows or pipelines There are many possible pipelines for a specific integration problem but there is not yet a general approach to evaluate the overall quality and performance of such pipelines to be able to determine the best choices. We therefore propose a new benchmark KGI-Bench to evaluate integration pipelines that ingest different kinds of input data into an existing KG. We evaluate pipelines by analyzing their output, i.e., the updated KG, with the three complementary quality metrics coverage, correctness and consistency. We also provide benchmark datasets (seed KG, overlapping input data of three formats, reference KG as a ground truth) for the movie domain. To demonstrate the applicability and usefulness of the proposed benchmark, we comparatively evaluate 12 pipelines and analyze their behavior across different input data formats and design choices.

摘要：整合新數據到知識圖譜 (KG) 通常涉及在工作流程或管道中執行的不同任務。對於特定的整合問題，有許多可能的管道，但目前尚未有一種通用的方法來評估這些管道的整體質量和性能，以便確定最佳選擇。因此，我們提出了一個新的基準 KGI-Bench，以評估將不同類型的輸入數據納入現有 KG 的整合管道。我們通過分析其輸出，即更新後的 KG，來評估管道，使用三個互補的質量指標：覆蓋率、正確性和一致性。我們還提供了電影領域的基準數據集（種子 KG、三種格式的重疊輸入數據、作為真實參考的 KG）。為了展示所提基準的適用性和實用性，我們比較評估了 12 條管道，並分析它們在不同輸入數據格式和設計選擇下的行為。

##### **SciCore-Mol: Augmenting Large Language Models with Pluggable Molecular Cognition Modules**
2605.22287v1 by Yuxuan Chen, Changwei Lv, Yunduo Xiao, Zhongjing Du, Daquan Zhou, Yukun Yan, Zheni Zeng, Zhiyuan Liu

Large Language Models (LLMs) are central to the one-for-all intelligent paradigm, but they face a fundamental challenge when dealing with heterogeneous scientific data such as molecules: the inherent gap between discrete linguistic symbols and topological molecular or continuous reaction data leads to significant information loss and semantic noise in text-based reasoning. We propose SciCore-Mol, a modular framework that bridges this gap through three deeply integrated pluggable cognitive modules: a topology-aware perception module, a latent diffusion-based molecular generation module, and a reaction-aware reasoning module. Each module is coupled to the LLM backbone through learned representation interfaces, enabling richer information exchange than is possible with text-only tool feedback. Our experiments on diverse chemical tasks demonstrate that SciCore-Mol achieves strong comprehensive performance across molecular understanding, generation, reaction prediction, and general chemistry knowledge, with an 8B-parameter open-source system that is competitive with and in several dimensions surpasses proprietary large models. This work provides a systematic blueprint for equipping LLMs with scientific expertise through decoupled, pluggable, and flexibly orchestrated modules, with direct implications for drug design, chemical synthesis, and broader scientific discovery.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在一體化智能範式中占據核心地位，但在處理異質科學數據（如分子）時面臨根本挑戰：離散語言符號與拓撲分子或連續反應數據之間的固有差距導致文本推理中的顯著信息損失和語義噪聲。我們提出了SciCore-Mol，一個模組化框架，通過三個深度集成的可插拔認知模組來彌合這一差距：一個拓撲感知感知模組、一個基於潛在擴散的分子生成模組，以及一個反應感知推理模組。每個模組都通過學習的表示接口與LLM主幹相連，實現比僅依賴文本工具反饋更豐富的信息交換。我們在多樣的化學任務上的實驗表明，SciCore-Mol在分子理解、生成、反應預測和一般化學知識方面實現了強大的綜合性能，並且這個擁有8B參數的開源系統在多個維度上與專有大型模型競爭並超越它們。這項工作為通過解耦、可插拔和靈活協調的模組為LLMs提供科學專業知識提供了一個系統性的藍圖，對藥物設計、化學合成和更廣泛的科學發現具有直接影響。

##### **Can Transformers Learn to Verify During Backtracking Search?**
2605.22221v1 by Yin Jun Phua, Tony Ribeiro, Tuan Nguyen, Katsumi Inoue

Backtracking search underlies classical constraint solvers, planners, and theorem provers. Recent transformer-based reasoning systems explore search trees over their own intermediate steps. A common training recipe fits an autoregressive next-token loss on offline solver traces. The model's input at each step is a cumulative trace of all prior decisions. The optimal continue-or-backtrack predictor depends only on the current search state, since two trajectories reaching the same state admit the same viable continuations. We show that decoder-only transformers trained on cumulative traces fail this requirement in two ways: the trace can scatter state features across many positions (scattered retrieval), and the predictor can condition on the trajectory rather than the state (history entanglement). We address scattered retrieval with localization, a trace-level fix that rewrites each decision block to expose state features locally. We address history entanglement with Selective State Attention (SSA), a fixed attention mask that enforces state-based decisions structurally without modifying training data, objective, or parameters. We focus on reactive verification, after propagation has exposed a contradiction. We test SSA on 3-SAT, graph coloring, Blocks World, and backtracking parsing. On same-state pairs that differ only in prior history, SSA emits identical decisions while a cumulative-trained causal baseline does not. Our contribution is a diagnostic of transformer behavior on serialized trajectory data, paired with a structural fix. Pretrained language models that search over their own reasoning steps may face the same failure. Our analysis opens up inference-time context clearing as a candidate way to apply the same isolation without retraining.

摘要：回溯搜索是傳統約束求解器、規劃者和定理證明者的基礎。最近的基於Transformer的推理系統探索其自身中間步驟的搜索樹。一個常見的訓練配方是在離線求解器的痕跡上擬合自回歸的下一個標記損失。模型在每一步的輸入是所有先前決策的累積痕跡。最佳的繼續或回溯預測器僅依賴於當前的搜索狀態，因為到達相同狀態的兩條軌跡允許相同的可行延續。我們展示了僅解碼器的Transformer在累積痕跡上訓練時在兩個方面未能滿足這一要求：痕跡可能在許多位置散佈狀態特徵（散佈檢索），而預測器可以基於軌跡而非狀態進行條件（歷史糾纏）。我們通過定位來解決散佈檢索，這是一種痕跡級別的修正，重寫每個決策區塊以局部顯示狀態特徵。我們通過選擇性狀態注意力（SSA）來解決歷史糾纏，這是一種固定的注意力掩碼，結構上強制基於狀態的決策，而不修改訓練數據、目標或參數。我們專注於反應性驗證，在傳播暴露出矛盾之後。我們在3-SAT、圖著色、方塊世界和回溯解析上測試SSA。在僅在先前歷史上有所不同的同狀態對中，SSA發出相同的決策，而累積訓練的因果基準則不然。我們的貢獻是對Transformer在序列化軌跡數據上的行為進行診斷，並配合結構性修正。搜索自身推理步驟的預訓練語言模型可能面臨相同的失敗。我們的分析開啟了推理時上下文清除作為應用相同隔離而不重新訓練的候選方法。

##### **Skill Weaving: Efficient LLM Improvement via Modular Skillpacks**
2605.22205v1 by Zhuo Li, Guodong Du, Zesheng Shi, Weiyang Guo, Weijun Yao, Yuan Zhou, Jiabo Zhang, Jing Li

Large language models increasingly require specialization across diverse domains, yet existing approaches struggle to balance multi-domain capacities with strict memory and inference constraints. In this work, we introduce SkillWeave, a modular improvement framework that enables LLMs to specialize under fixed memory budgets. SkillWeave partitions full capabilities of a general-purpose model into skillpacks -- lightweight, domain-specific delta modules -- that reorganize and refine the model's internal knowledge. For efficient deployment, SkillWeave integrates SkillZip to compress skillpacks into compact and inference-ready format, enabling strong multi-domain performance with low-latency execution. On multi-task and agentic benchmarks, a 9B SkillWeave model outperforms several baselines and even surpasses a 32B monolithic LLM, while achieving up to 4x speedup.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越需要在多樣化領域中專業化，但現有的方法在平衡多領域能力與嚴格的記憶和推理限制方面面臨挑戰。在這項工作中，我們介紹了SkillWeave，一個模組化的改進框架，使LLM能夠在固定的記憶預算下專業化。SkillWeave將通用模型的完整能力劃分為技能包——輕量級的特定領域增量模組——這些模組重新組織和精煉模型的內部知識。為了高效部署，SkillWeave整合了SkillZip，將技能包壓縮為緊湊且準備好推理的格式，從而實現強大的多領域性能和低延遲執行。在多任務和代理基準測試中，一個9B的SkillWeave模型超越了幾個基準，甚至超過了一個32B的單體LLM，同時實現了高達4倍的加速。

##### **Maestro: Reinforcement Learning to Orchestrate Hierarchical Model-Skill Ensembles**
2605.22177v1 by Jinyang Wu, Guocheng Zhai, Ruihan Jin, Yuhao Shen, Zhengxi Lu, Fan Zhang, Haoran Luo, Zheng Lian, Zhengqi Wen, Jianhua Tao

The proliferation of large language models (LLMs) and modular skills has endowed autonomous agents with increasingly powerful capabilities. Existing frameworks typically rely on monolithic LLMs and fixed logic to interface with these skills. This gives rise to a critical bottleneck: different LLMs offer distinct advantages across diverse domains, yet current frameworks fail to exploit the complementary strengths of models and skills, thereby limiting their performance on downstream tasks. In this paper, we present Maestro (Multimodal Agent for Expert-Skill Targeted Reinforced Orchestration), a Reinforcement Learning (RL)-driven orchestration framework that reframes heterogeneous multimodal tasks as a sequential decision-making process over a hierarchical model-skill registry. Rather than consolidating all knowledge into a single model, Maestro trains a lightweight policy to dynamically compose ensembles of frozen expert models and a two-tier skill library, deciding at each step whether to invoke an external expert, which model-skill pair to select, and when to terminate. The policy is optimized via outcome-based RL, requiring no step-level supervision. We evaluate Maestro across ten representative multimodal benchmarks spanning mathematical reasoning, chart understanding, high-resolution perception, and domain-specific analysis. With only a 4B orchestrator, Maestro achieves an average accuracy of 70.1%, surpassing both GPT-5 (69.3%) and Gemini-2.5-Pro (68.7%). Crucially, the learned coordination policy generalizes to unseen models and skills without retraining: augmenting the registry with out-of-domain experts yields a 59.5% average on four challenging benchmarks, outperforming all closed-source baselines. Maestro further maintains high computational efficiency with low latency. The source code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/Maestro.

摘要：大型語言模型 (LLMs) 和模組化技能的增長，使自主代理擁有了越來越強大的能力。現有的框架通常依賴於單一的 LLM 和固定的邏輯來與這些技能進行接口。這產生了一個關鍵瓶頸：不同的 LLM 在多樣的領域中提供了不同的優勢，但當前的框架未能利用模型和技能的互補優勢，從而限制了它們在下游任務中的表現。在本文中，我們提出了 Maestro（專家技能針對性強化編排的多模態代理），這是一個基於強化學習 (RL) 的編排框架，將異質的多模態任務重新構建為一個在層次模型-技能註冊表上的序列決策過程。Maestro 並不是將所有知識整合到一個單一模型中，而是訓練一個輕量級的策略，動態組合凍結的專家模型和雙層技能庫，在每一步決定是否調用外部專家、選擇哪個模型-技能對以及何時終止。該策略通過基於結果的 RL 進行優化，無需逐步監督。我們在十個具有代表性的多模態基準上評估 Maestro，涵蓋數學推理、圖表理解、高解析度感知和特定領域分析。僅用 4B 的編排器，Maestro 實現了 70.1% 的平均準確率，超越了 GPT-5（69.3%）和 Gemini-2.5-Pro（68.7%）。關鍵是，學習到的協調策略在未見過的模型和技能上具有良好的泛化能力，無需重新訓練：將註冊表擴充至域外專家，在四個具有挑戰性的基準上達到 59.5% 的平均值，超越了所有封閉源基準。Maestro 還保持了高計算效率和低延遲。源代碼可在 https://github.com/jinyangwu/Maestro 獲得。

##### **Do Factual Recall Mechanisms Carry over from Text to Speech in Multimodal Language Models?**
2605.22170v1 by Luca Modica, Filip Landin, Mehrdad Farahani, Livia Qian, Gabriel Skantze, Richard Johansson

In recent years, several Speech Language Models (SLMs) that represent speech and written text jointly have been presented. The question then emerges about how model-internal mechanisms are similar and different when operating in the two modalities. We focus on how these systems encode, store, and retrieve factual knowledge, which has previously been investigated for text-only models. To investigate mechanisms behind the storage and recall of factual association in SLMs, we leverage Causal Mediation Analysis, a technique previously applied to text-based models.
